

[Private and Confidential. —Not for Publication.
GENERAL ORDER No. 27/1916.]
NEW ZEALAND EXPEDITIONARY FORCE
BOOK XIII.
LIST OF CASUALTIES
AND A
SUMMARY OF CASUALTIES
IN ORDER OF UNITS
Reported from the 15th May, 1918, to the 14th August, 1918.
ALSO INCLUDING A COMPLETE
SUMMARY OF ALL CASUALTIES
IN THEIR RESPECTIVE UNITS
Up to and including 14th August, 1918.
WELLINGTON.
AUTHORITY \ MARCUS F. MARKS, GOVERNMENT PRINTER.
